KA JINGIM BAD JINGTREl U TRAl JISU. la ka jingim bad jingtrci U Trai Jisu lah ban thoh lyngkot lang khyndial ki laiii. katba ngi lah ban him na ki jingthoh |ong ki sawngut ki nongthoh Gospel. Kine ki nongthoh ki la thoh shen hadien U Trai Jisu hapdeng ki snem laiphew haduh hynriewphew', bad baroh kaba ki la thoh ka long Shaphang ka jaka khaiia U (Mik. 5:2; nujor Math. 2:1). kham bun kaba ki la iohi da la ki khmat bad ba ki la ioh- sngcw da 1 1 ki shkor. la la don napdeng jong ki kiba la thoh da kaba iohsngcw pateng na ki synran U Trai Jisu hi. La kha ia U Jisu ha u bnai December ka snem kaba 5 ha shnong Bethlehem, Judia, hynriew mail shathie na Jerusalem. Na Bethlehem ki kmic ki kpa U Jisu ki la phct sha ri Ijipt namar ba u Herod Syiem u la wad ban pyniap ia U Jisu. Hadien tang khyndiat por ki la wan phai ban shong sha Nasareth, ka shnong trai jong ka Mari bad u Joseph ynda haba ki la iohsngcw ba u Herod u la iap. Dei hangne ba U Jisu U la san U la rangbah kum u khun misteri haduh ba U la dap 30 snem ka rta. Hapdeng kine ki snem ym 66 don jingtip ei ei shuh lait tang ha ka por ba U la dap 12!' snem ba U la don hapoh ka Tempi ha Jerusalem. Haba U la dap 30 snem ka rta U la mih na Nasareth ban leit shah pynbaptis ha u loannis Nongpynbaptis ha ka wah Jordan. Nangta pat U la don ha ri khlaw ban shah pynshoi da u Soitan. Na ri khlaw U iaid harud ka Duriaw Galilaia ha kaba U la khot hynriew ngut na ki synran jong U — u Jakob, u loannis, u Andriw, u Simon Petros, u Philip bad u Nathanail, bad shen hadien nangne pat u khot shuh shuh sa hynriew ngut ban bud ia U. Nangta pat U la pynlut katto katne por ban hikai bad ban pynkhiah harud kane ka Duriaw, U sa leit sha Jerusalem ha ka Niam ka Jinglait. Naduh kanc ka por haduh hynriew bnai shuwa ka jing- shah sahnarphna ia U ka long kaba eh ban da buh thikna ia ka por. Ka ktien Grik ka la long ka ktien kaba iasngewthuh paidbah. Kane ka pynsuk ia U Trai Jisu ban kren, ban hikai bad ban iaiap ia ka Gospel. (3) Kawei pat ka jingpynkhreh ka la long na ka liang ka ioh ka duh (Economics). Imat kumba arngut na ki laingut ki nongshong; shnong ha ri Palestain ha kane ka por ki la long ki shakri lane ki mraw jong ka Sorkar. Ki Synran U Trai Jisu: U Trai Jisu U la khot 12 ngut ki synran jong U ban sakhi ia ka jingim bad jingtrei jong U ; lah ruh bun ong ban mihkhmat na ka bynta ki 12 Jail Israel, bad la seng ruh ia ka Balang halor jong ki (Jingpyn. 21 :12-I4). Laingut ki nongthoh Gospel-Vfathaios, Mark os, Loukas— ki Ihoh ia ki kyrteng kine ki synran, bad kumjuh ruh la shem ha ki Kam ki Apostol (Pule Math. 10:2-4 ; Mark. 3:16-19 ; Louk. 6:12-19 ; Ki Kam 1:13). Lah ban thoh lyngkot ia ka jingim ki synran uwei pa iiwei kumne harum :— (\) U Simon— V dei u khun u Jonah, la khot ruh ia u u Kephas ne u Petros, kaba mut ‘U Mawsiang’. U la thoh artylli ki Shithi, [ bad II Petros. U la iarap ruh lehse ia u Markos 71 ban thoh ia ka Gospel. U dei u mishoneri hapdeng ki Jiw ha Babilon bad ruh haduh ha Rom. Ka shnong trai jong ki ka dei na Belhsaid'i bad nangta ki la kynriah sha Jerusalem ; baroh arngut ki dei ki nongtong dohkha. U Jakob u la ialap ha Judia bad ha Jerusalem. Ki Pharshi U Trai Jisu: U Jisu U Ju kren da ki pharshi habrt U hikai. o kren da kiei kiei kiba lah ban iohi ne kiba lah ban tip ban batai ne ai nuksa ia kiei kiei kiba jylliew bad kiba kynja mynsiem. Ban shu ong lyngkot : Ki Pharshi ki long ki Jingiathuh- khana lyngkot ba la shim nuksa ia kiei kiei kiba shisha. Ka jinglong Syiem bad ka Hitia U Jisu ki long ki bym lah ban peiphang ia ka jingsngewthuh briew, ■ namarkata U ong ka Hima U Blci ka long kum kane bad katai da ki pharshi khnang ba ki briew kin sngewthuh. Ka long kaba eh ban da buh thikna ia ki nombar jong ki pharshi, namar don nih na ki kiba ngim lah ban ong ba ki dei ki pharshi, hynrei tang ki kynja Proberb (jingkren ki newstod), kum “Ka jaifi kaba rim bad ka jaifl kaba thym- mat , Ka sbarak ha ka dieog pynieng sharak”. Don 77 pat kiba long tang ki metaphor (ki rukom kren ba don jing- mut) kum “Ki langbrot bad ki blang”, “Ka ling halor u mawsiang bad ka i'ing halor u shyiap”. La kumno kumno ruh ki pharshi U Trai Jisu ki pynshisha ba U long U Riew^ stad Uba khraw eh bad U Nonghikai Uba na bneng ; nangta ruh ngi shem ba ki pharshi ba U la kren ki ai jingUkai ha kano kano ka por bad lah ban pyndei ia ki ha kano kano ka rukom. Kiba kham bun na kine ki pharshi ki dei shaphang ka Hima U BIci ne ka Hima ki bneng. Hynrei lah ban pyniakhlad ia ki ha ki katto katne ki bynta (groups) : (1) Ki pharshi shaphang ka jingsdang bad ka jingroi ka Hima U Blei, kum ka pharshi u Symbai Tyrso, u Symbai ba la bet. (2) Ki pharshi shaphang ka jingduwai, kum u Lok shiteng synfiia, it Pharisi bad u Nongkhrong. (3) Ki pharshi sha* pl'.ang ka jinglong jingim ki briew, kum u nong Samaria uba bha, u Sordar uba stad. (4) Ki pharshi shaphang ka jing* ieit bah U Biei. kum u Khun Sarong Awria, Ka ’Langbrot ba la jah noh. (5) Ki pharshi shaphang ka jingwan pat U Jisu Khrist ; kum ki shiphew ngut ki Theisotti, ka jing- khawai shongkurim u khun syiem. (6) Ki pharshi shaphang ka bainong lawei jong kiba hok bad ki bymhok ; kum uba ricwspah bad u Lasaros, ki ’Langbrot bad ki Blang. Hangne harum ngin kdew ia ki pharshi baroh bad ban pyrshang buh ruh ia ka jinghikai kaba mih na ka jingmut jong kawei pa kawei ka pharshi. ( I) Ba la thoh ha kawei ka Gospel. KA RI PALESTAIN. Ka Ri Palestain ka dei ka ri ka jingkular U Blei ia U Abraham bad ki khun ki ksiew jong u pateng la pateng. 1. (a) Ki kyrteng Jong kane ka ri: (1) La khot ia ka ka Ri Kanaan (Gen. 16:3; 17:8). La pyndonkam ia kane ka kyrteng ha ka por shuwa ba ki briew jong U Blei ki wan shong. (2) Ka Israel (TI Syiem 5:2). Ia kane ka kyrteng la pyndonkam naduh ka por ba ki Israel ki la shong haduh ka por ba la ringmraw ia ki sha Babilon. (3) La khot ruh ka Judah (Neh. 5:4; Mark. 1:5). la kane ka kyrteng la khot hadien ba ki la wan phai na ka jing- longmraw. La khot Judah bad Israel : kawei ka daw ka long namar ka jingiapait hima jong ki syiem ha ka por u Rehoboam ; ia ki arjait Judah bad Benjamin la khot Judah bad ia ki syiem la khot ki syiem Judah. Ka dei ka bynta kaba sha- thie jong ka ri. la ka bynta jong ki shiphew jait kaba sha- phang shatei la khot Israel bad ia ki syiem la khot ki syiem Israel. (4) La khot ruh ia kane ka ri ka ri Palestain. La shem ia kane ka kyrteng ha Joel 3.4, bad ka wan mih na ka ktien Philistain; hynrei naduh ka por uta u nongthoh Histori uba kyrteng u Jesephos, la khot ia ka ka Palestain. la kane ka kyrteng Palestain la pyndonkam ha ka por U Trai Jisu bad haduh mynta ruh, tangba ha ka por U Jisu Khrist hapoh ka jingsynshar ki nong-Rom la pyniabynta ia ka ha ki 5 bynta : — (1) Ka Ri Galilaia ka don shaphang shatei bad ka heh kumba 1600 mail sawdong. (2) Ka Ri Samaria ka don hapdeng bad kane ka heh 1400 mail saw- dong. (3) Ka Ri Judia, shathie na Samaria, ka heh 2000 mail sawdong. (4) Ka Tetrakhy u Herod Philip, kane ka don 99 sha mihngi na Galilaia bad shatei na Perea. (5) Ka Ri Perea ka don shathie na ka Tetrakhy u Herod Philip, sha mihngi na Samaria bad Judia ba la pyniakhlad da ka wah Jordan. (b) Ki pud sawdong jong ka ri Palestain : Shaphang shatei — Ka Syro Phoinicia bad Lum Hermon. Shaphang shathie— Ka Ri Khlaw Judia bad Duriaw Basaw. Shaphang mihngi— Persia bad ka ri shyiap Arabia. Shaphang sepngi — Ka Duriaw Bakhraw. Ka Ri Palestain — Ka lynter jong ka ka long kumba 140 mail, ka pyngkiang kumba 40 mail shatei, bad kumba 70 mail shaphang shathie. (k) Ka jinglong kane ka ri: Kane ka ri Palestain haba ong kyllum ka long ha ki saw rukom ka jinglong jong ka : (I) Ka bynta kaba sha sepngi naduh shatei haduh shathie ka dei ka madan rud duriaw jong ka Duriaw Bakhraw. Ka long ka jaka kaba seisoh bad bun ki shnong khai'i ki don harud ka Duriaw. (2) Nangta pat bud sa ka jaka ri lum ba pyngngad na shatei haduh shathie. Ka nongbah Jerusalem ka don hapdeng kine ki lynter Lum. (3) Ka jaka ri them ba seisoh jong ka wah Jordan baroh arliang. (4) Ki lynter lum mihngi. Kane ka ri ka paw pyrthei lyngba kine ki snem : (1) Naduh ba sdang haduh ka jingjop da u Joshua kumba 470 snem. (2) Naduh ka por u Joshua haduh ka jingpait hima kumba 476 snem. (3) Naduh ka jingpait hima haduh ka jingwanphai na ka jinglong mraw 566 snem . (4) Naduh ka jingwanphai na ka jinglong mraw haduh ka por ka jingjot ka Jerusalem (70 S.K.) ka long kumba 490 snem ; kata ka mut ka ri ka la don ha ka kti ki Israel kumba arbajar snem. 100 2. Ki Nongsynshar ia ka ri Palestain : Hapoh ka jingsynshar ki Nongbishar hadien ka jing- pynbynta u Joshua ha ki khadar jait, ka jingsynshar kam da iaid ryntih eh, hynrei naduh ba u Samuel u la thung ia u Saul, nangta ia u Dabid ban long syiem, bad nangta pat bud sa u Solomon Syiem, ka ri Kanaan ne ka Hima Israel ka la long kawei na ki hima kiba khraw hapoh Asia. Hadien u Solomon ka hima ka la pait arliang ba la khot ka Hima Judah bad ka Hima Israel. Ha kane ka por la don bun ki syiem bad ki non^hun ruh kumba laispah snem. Kumta namar ba ki syiem ki long kiba tlot la jop ia ki da ki nong- Babilon ha ka 600 S.K. bad la ring mraw ia ki sha Babilon. Ha ka jingjop Jong u Sairos ia ka Babilon la shah ia ki Jiw ban leit phai pat sha Palestain hapoh ka jingialam u Ne- hemaiah, u Esra, u Serobbabel. Kumta ka ri Palestain ka la sah hapoh ki syiem Medo-Persia haduh ka jingwan jop pat da u Aleksander uba khraw jong ka ri Kris (Greece). Hadien nan^a pat la mih uwei u syiem Syria uba kyrteng u Antiokhus Epiphanes ha ka snem 170 S.K. ia uba la khot u Khrist Lamler ka Testament Barim, bad namar ba kirn sngewbha ia ka jinglong jong u, u la kut jingmut ban pynduh ia ka Niam Jiw. U leit sha Jerusalem u da shna ia ka dur bleithaw Jupiter ban buh hapoh ka jaka kyntang tarn, bad u hukum ban kgia da ki sniang hapoh ka Tempi. U dawa ia u Mathathias u lyngdoh ki Jiw ban ai jingk/jia ha ki bleithaw. Une u Mathathias ha ka jaka ban kohnguh ia une u syiem runar u la pyniap ia u nongrah khubor syiem bad nangta ma u bad ki khun jong u ki la phet sha ri khlaw. Ki khun utei u lyngdoh ki la lum lang ia ki Jiw ha ka snem (168 S.K.) ban ialeh pyrshah ia utei u syiem. Ha ka snem 165 S.K. u Judas Makabaios, uwei na ki khun u Mathathias, u la jop ia ki Syria bad u la pynkhuid ia ka Tempi. Kane ka dei ka jingsdang jong ka jingrakhe ia ka niam ka jing- pynkhuid (loan. 10:22). Ki khun u Makabaios ba la khot Makabi ki la synshar kumba 100 snem. U Hirekanos u dei u syiem uba khatduh eh ha kaba la pyniap bad la wan jop da u Herod Bakhraw. 101 3. Ka jait sykm Herod: Kumba ngi la tip hadien u Hirekamos la synshar ia ka ri Palestain da u Herod Bakhraw, bad hadien une u Herod sa ki khun jong u. Kine ki Herod kirn dei na ka jait Jiw hynrei ki long ki nong-Idumia. Khnang ban lAam tip ia ki baroh ngin thoh lyngkot ia ki uwei pa uwei : — (1) U Herod I lane n Herod Bakhraw— U dei u khun u Antipeter lane u Antipas. La pynsan pynrangbah ia u kum u Jiw ha ka por ba u Hirekanos u dang synshar ia ka Idumia. Ha ka snem 47 S.K. ia u kpa jong u la thung lyng- skor da u Julius Kaisar; namarkata, ka kam ka la hiar haduh ha ki khun ruh. U Herod u la sdang ban long syiem ha Judia ha ka snem 40 S.K. U la long u nongsynshar uba khlaiii. U la tei ia ka Tempi ha Jerusalem ha ka snem 20 S. K. Hynrei dei une ruh uba la phah pyniap ia ki khuniung kiba arsnem bad kiba kham poh da kaba pyrkhat ba U Jisu ruh Un iap, namar ka jingshep- tieng ba ioh U Jisu Un long U Syiem, hynrei U Khuniung Jisu U la lait im da kaba ki kmie ki kpa jong U ki la ialam ban phet sha ri Ijipt. U la pyniap ruh ia ki rangbah ka Durbar Sanhedrin baroh lait sa tang arngut. U Herod I u la don 10 ngut ki tnga bad shibun ki khun. U la ioh ka jingpang ba shyrkhei bad kumta la ong ba u la phah siat iap ia lade ha ka snem 4 S.K. (2) U Herod Antipas — U dei u Herod uba long u khun u Herod Bakhraw na ka tnga jong u kaba long ka nong- Samaria. U Antipas u la long u Tetrak jong ka Galilaia bad Persia, bad u la shim tnga da ka khun u syiem Arabia, Hynrei u la klim ia ka Herodia ka tnga u Philip u para jong u, bad na kane ka daw u la set byndi bad khrai khlieh ia u loannis Nongpynbaptis. U la long uba iajan eh bad u Patsha Tiberios ; namarkata u la tei nam ia ka shnong Tiberias ha ka kyrteng u Tiberios. Ha ka snem 38 S.K. la pynryngkang par ia u sha Lungdumnum kaba ha ri Gaul bad u la iap pat ha ri Spain. 102 (3) U Herod Arkhelos — Une ruh u dei u khun jong u Herod Bakhraw hi. U la long u hynmen jong u Herod Antipas ; namarkata la thung syiem ia u ha Judia. La don ka jingpyrshah da ki paidbah ba kim mon ia u ban long syiem ha Judia. Ki paidbah ki la apil haduh u Patsha ha Rom, hynrei u Herod Arkhelos u la leit da lade sha Rom ban pynskhem ia ka jinglong syiem jong u. Pynban ha ka snem 6 H.K. la pynryngkang par ia u sha Vienna ha Gaul bad ia ka Judia pat la buh hapoh ka jingsynshar beit na Rom hapoh ka jingpeit ki Lyngskor. Kumta ha ka por U Jisu Khrist dei u Pontios Pilat uba long u Lyngskor ka Judia, ka jingsynshar ki Lyngskor ka la neh haduh ka snem 41 H.K. (4) U Herod Philip 1 — La khot ia u u Herod Philip da u Jesephos u nongthoh histori, katba ha ki Gospel la shu khot ia u tang u Philip (Math. 14:3; Mark. 6:17 bad Louk. 3:1). U dei u khun u Herod Bakhraw na ka tnga jong u kaba kyrteng ka Mariam, ka khun u Simon Rangbah Lyngdoh. Namar ka jingshun ka kmie jong u, u la iehnoh ia ka kam da kaba phet sha Rom. Une u dei u tnga ka Herodia kaba la iaklim bad u Herod Antipas. (5) U Philip II — Une ruh u dei u khun u Herod Bakhraw na ka Kleopatra, ka tnga jong u. La pynsan pynrangbah ia u ryngkat bad u Arkhelos, u Antipas. Une u la long u Tetrak ka Batania, ka Trakhonitis bad ka Aranitis. U Loukas u thoh ba u dei ruh u Tetrak ka Itunia bad ka Tra- khonitis. Une u la synshar naduh 4 S.K. haduh 34 H.K. U la long u nongsynshar uba bha bad uba hok. U la tei ia ka nongbah Kaisaria Philipi bad Bethsaida. Ka tnga jong u, ka Salomi, ka dei ka khun u Herod Philip I na ka Herodia ka tnga klim. Te namar ba um don khun, ia ka hima jong u la pyniasoh bad ka jylla Syria kaba dei ka jong ki nong-Rom. Ka Herodia (Math. 14:1; Mark. 6:14; Louk. 3:19) ka la long ka khun u khun u Herod Bakhraw uba kyrteng 103 u Aristubulos bad ka Bernis ka tnga jong u. Nyngkong ka la iashong bad u Herod Philip I bad nangta ka la ioh ka khun kynthei kaba kyrteng ka Salomi. Dei kane kaba la shad ha khmat u Herod Antipas ban pynsngewbha ia u. Ka Herodia ka la bthah ruh ia la ka khun ba kan pan ia ka khlieh u loannis Nongpynbaptis namar ba u pynrem ia ka jingiashong sang jong ki. Kumta ka Herodia ka pyllait ia u Herod Philip I da kaba iashong bad u Herod Antipas. Namar ka pop jong ki la ringmraw ia ki baroh arngut sha Lyons ha ri Gaul. (6) U Agrippa I — La khot ia u, u Agrippa I uba khraw da u Jesephos. U dei u khun u khun u Herod uba kyrteng u Aristubulos bad ka Bernis ka tnga jong u. Ka Herodia ka dei ka para jong u Agrippa I. Ia u Agrippa ia pynsan pynrangbah ha Rom. Ha ka por ba u Kaligula u la long u Patsha ha Rom ha ka snem 37 H.K., la thung ia u Agrippa ban long u syiem ha ka jaka u Philip uba la iap. Ha ka snem 38 H.K. la ai synshar ruh ha u ia ka Galilaia bad Perea ka jaka u Antipas. Nangta pat ha ka snem 41 H.K. la ai shuh shuh sa ia ka Judia biad ka Samaria, bad kumta la khot ia u da ka nam syiem. Namarkata u la long uba khraw syriem kum u kparad jong u, u Herod Bakhraw. U shong ha Jerusalem u da sumar pyrkhing ia ki Hukum u Moses. Um shah ba kawei ruh ka sngi kan sep khlem da ioh ban knia ainguh. Kane ka jingim pyrkhing jong u ka la pyn* long ia u ba un iapyrshah ia ka Balang ha ki sngi ki Apostol (Ki Kara. 12). U la iap ha ka snem 44 H.K. Ka kyrteng ka tnga jong u, ka Kaipros, ka la pynkha ia u Agrippa 11, ka Bernis bad ka Drosilla. (7) U Agrippa II — U khun u Herod Agrippa I. U dang 17 snem ka rta haba u kpa jong u u la iap, kumta u Patsha Klaudios u la peit hi shipor na Rom ia ka hima u kpa jong u. Ha ka snem 48 H.K. la ai synshar ia u Agrippa II ia ka Khaldis, bad ha ka snem S3 H.K. la ai peit ruh ia ka Lysinias bad la pynkup ruh ha u ia ka nam syiem. Ha 104 ka por u Patsha Nero la ai synshar ruh ha u ia ka Galilaia bad ka Persia. U Agrippa II u la shong ha Kaisaria Phi- lip!. U la pyniadei ia lade bad ki patsha Rom. Kumta u la nangkhraw ha ka burom. la ki sngi kiba khatduh jong u, u la pynlut ha Rom. U la iap lehse ha ka snem 100 H.K. bad la pynkut artad ia ka jait Herod. 4. Ki Nongialam ha ka ri ha ka por II Jisu Khrist: Ha ka por U Trai Jisu ki don katto katne ki kynhun hapdeng ki Jiw kiba don la ka jong ka jong ka jingngeit bad ka jinglong jingim, hynrei kiba la iasoh lang ha kaba wad daw ban pyniap ia U Jisu. Kita ki long : — (1) Ki Pharisi (kiba la pynkyrpang). Kane ka kyn- hun ka la mih lehse na ki kynja jingkfdh bad ki kynja rebai- bal. Ki la long ka kynhun ba kham bun paid. Ki ialeh ban sumar pyrkhing bad bniah ruh ia ki Hukum U Blei. Ki ngeit ba ki Hukum ba U Blei U la ai ha u Moses la pyn- janai ia ki da ki jingiathuhkhana pateng. Kane ka kynhun ka la sdang ban mih ynda hadien ba ki Jiw ki la wan phai na ka jinglong mraw na Babilon. Ki briew baroh ki burom ia ki namar ba ki la leh riewblei ia lade. Ki jinghikai jong ki ki long kumne : — (a) Ki ngeit ba ki Hukum kiba hiar pateng ki iaryngkat dor bad ki Hukum ba shisha U Blei. (b) Da kaba sumar ia kine ki Hukum baroh ar — kin ioh ksan ha khmat U Blei ; yn lum lang ia ki kam ba bha jong ki baroh. (k) Ki ngeit ia ki kam kiba sh^bar kum kaba shah jingit, kaba ai isynei, kaba duwai jlan, kaba phla pop, ki long ka kuna namar ki pop. (d) Ki ngeit ba ki jingmut bad ki jingpyrkhat kirn long pop lada ym da leh ia ki ha ki kam. (e) Shaphang ka jingmihpat ki ngeit, bad ba don ka bainong ia kiba hok bad kiba pop. Ki don ruh ki Angel kiba bha bad ki Angel ba sniew. Kine kim da suidfiiew eh ia ka jingkylla kaba mut kaba shisha ; ki long ki riewarsap, lu nongpyndep rukom bad 105 ki im jingmut tang ia kiei kiei kiba shabar. Na kane ka jinglong jong ki U Jisu Um sngewtynnad ia ki ; naniarkata ki la iawad daw ban pyniap ia U, lem bad kiwei kiwei ki kynhun. (2) Ki Sadusi— La ngeit ba kime ki la hiar pateng na u Sadok uba long u Rangbah Lyngdoh ha ka por u Dabid bad u Solomon. Ka kyrteng Sadusi kam don ha ka Gospel u loannis bad ha ki Shithi. La katta ruh ka long kawei na ki kynhun niam kaba khlaifi shibun. Ki dei kyn- hun kaba kynthup ia ki riewnang riewstad, kiba riewspah bad kiba donburom. Ha shuwa U Jisu Khrist kine ki la kwah ban long nongsynshar hapdeng ki Jiw, hynrei kim don ka bor ban ring ia u paidbah. Kine ki iapiter na ka jingngeit bad jinglong ki Pharisi bad wat pyrshah ruh ia ki jinghikai U Khrist. Namarkata U Jisu U pynrera ia ki ha kaba paw. Kine ki Sadusi ki len ia ka jingmihpat, ki len ia ka jingdon ki Angel, ki pdiang tang ia ki Kitab u Moses hynrei ki kyntait ia kiwei pat ki bynta ka ktien U Blei. Dei kine ruh kiba la iasylla ban pyniap noh ia (J Jisu ryng- kat bad kiwei ki kynhun. Ki Rangbah Lyngdoh ha ka por U Jisu ki dei na ka kynhun Sadusi. (3) Ki Nongthoh — Ki dei kiba nang ba stad bad ki kynja nonghikai ha ki Synagog. Ki long ki riewpule bad ki riew-U bniah ia ki Jingthoh Bakhuid. Don napdeng jong ki kiba long ki nongbishar wat ha iingkashari ruh. Ka kam kaba kham kongsan jong ki ka long ban pule, ban batai bad ban thoh ia ka Ktien U Blei. U Esra u nong- thoh ba pawnam u dei na kane ka kynhun. Hadien haba ki Israel ki la klet noh ia ka ktien Hebru bad ba ki la kren da ka Aramaik, kine ki nongthoh ki la hikai ia u paidbah da kaba pyntyllep noh ia ki Hukum kiba shisha U Blei da kine ki jinghikai hiar pateng. Na kane ka daw U Jisu U pynrem ia ki (Math. 15:1-9). Ki Nongthoh ki la long ruh ki dkhot ka Durbar ki Jiw ba la khot Sanhedrin. 106 (4) Ki Nongkhrong — Kine ki del ki nonglum khajna ha ka hima Rom (Math. 28:17). Kiwei pat ki kynhun ki isih ia ka rukom khrong khajna, bad ki da giewbein nih ia ki bad kirn shah ia ki ban rung wat hapoh ki Synagog bad ka Tempi. Ki long ki lok Jong kito kiba la shah kyn- tait bad kiba la niewbeifi. la U Jisu ruh la khot “U Lok ki nongkhrong bad kiba pop”, namar U shait ialok bad ki, U iabam iadih ruh bad ki. (5) Kiba Shitrhem — Kine ki long ki nongialeh pyr- shah ia ka Sorkar bad ia ki nongkhrong. Kim mon ban slew khajna ki da fliewbeifl ruh ia U Jisu. Uwei na ki synran U Jisu la khot ia u u Simon ba shitrhem (Louk. 6:15). Kane ka kynhun ka la mih ha ka snem 6 H.K. U Jisu U sngew- bha ban Jied synran wat napdeng kine ruh. (6) Ki Nongbud u Herod — Kine ki dei kiba iajan bad kyrshan ha iap ha im ia ka Jait syiem u Herod. Ki dei ki Jiw ha ki Jin^eh ba shabar hynrei ki im bad ki long kum ki Gentil. Ki long shibynta ka kynhun niam bad shibynta ka kynhun nongsynshar, ki da iapyrshah eh ia ki Pharisi bad ki Sadusi. La katta ruh ha ka Jingiapyrshah ia U Jisu ki la iadei Jingmut lang bad ki ialong kawei (Math. 22:16; Mark. 3:6; 12:13). U Jisu U maham ia ki synran ban kiar na ki rukom bad Jinglong Jong ki. (Mark. 8:15). (7) Ki Nasar-— (Ba la pyniakhlad ne pyniakyrpang). Kine ki don ar rukom : (a) kiba la aiti da ki kmie ki kpa naduh ba dang khunlung kum u Samson, u Samuel bad u loannis Nongpynbaptis ; (b) kiba shu aiti ia lade shi por ne shi rta. Ki Nasar ki long ki briew kiba kyndiah noh na ka waifi bad ka kiad ; ban ym dih ia ka um sohwaiji bad ka waifi kaba Jew ; ban ym bam ia u sohwain ba im ne uba la thad. Ka syrti kan ym dei ia ka khlich Jong ki ; kim shah ia ka Jingsan u shfiiuh Jong ki. Kin ym pynjan ia ka met iap. Kin ym pyntngit ia lade. Kane ka pyni ia ka bor synshar ia la ka mon ban aiti lut ha ka kam U Blei. 107 (8) Ki Essenes — Kine ruh ki long kiba la iehnoh lut ia ki jingsngewbha ka pyrthei baroh. Kim ju shongkurim, lymne dih lymne pyndonkam ia ka umphniang. Ki pyn> kyntang ia la ka jingim bad ia ka por baroh ban pule ia ki Jingthoh fiakhuid bad ia ki Ain u Moses. Ki pynlut por ruh ha kaba duwai, ha kaba rwai bad ha kaba lehsbun leh isynei. LYNNONG X. HADIEN U TRAI JISU. Ha kane ka lynnong ngin pynlut khamtam ia ki jing- jia bad ka jingroi ka Balang lyngba ki Apostol kumjuh ruh da u Paul, katba ngi lah ban shem khamtam eh na ka Kitab ki Kam ki Apostol. Kumba U Trai Jisu U la kular ban phah ia U Mynsiem Bakhuid ha la ki synran, bad ba kin iai ap ruh ha Jerusalem, kumta ki synran ki la ap haduh ka sngi Pentekost ha kaba la don bun ki paidbah ; bad U Myn* siem U Blei U la wan hiar bad U la ai bor halor uwei pa uwei na ki. Namar ka jingtrci ba phylla U Mynsiem Ba- khuid la kylla kaba mut ha kata ka sngi Pentekost kumba 3000 ngut, bad u Petros u la iathuhkhana ban pynshisha ba ka dei ka jingtrei U Mynsiem Bakhuid ba la kular da U Trai Jisu Uba la kiew sha bneng. Kumta ki la iasoh lang na ka por sha ka por ban pynlong jingiaseng, ban duwai ban ialap bad ban ai ruh sha ka kam U Blei. Ia ka Balang ha Jerusalem imat la seng hapdeng ki snem 29-30 H.K., katba ngi lah ban tip da kaba pule ia ki Kam 1:1-8. Hadien ka sngi Pentekost ki dkhot ka Sanhe- drin ki la iapyrshah ia ki Apostol, la ki Apostol kim shym sheptieng ia ki. Ki synran ki la thung pyndap ia u Mathias ban long u Apostol ha ka jaka u Judas uba la die noh ia la U Trai. Nangta ruh haba la man bun ki Khristan ki la thung sa hynniew ngut ki tymmenbasan, bad ia uwei na kine ki hynfiiew ngut uba kyrteng u Stephan la lynthem maw da ki kine ki paidbah kiba khih pyrshah. Ki Apostol 108 ki la iamih ban leit ialap ban pynkhiah ia kiba pang. U Philip u ialap ha Samaria, u Petros, u loannis bad kiwei ha Jerusalem; bad la pynbaptis ia u Komilios bad ka iing jong u. Nangta pat de U Trai Jisu U la paw ha u Saul, uwei na ki riew runar, ban long u atiar ka Gospel jong U. Shen liadicn nangne u Paul bad u Barnabas ki la mih ban leit ialap ia ka Gospel bad ban scng ia ki Baking Jentil. La seng ia ka Balang ha Antiok lolisc ha ka sncm 42 H.K. Ka Durbar Khristan kaba nyngkong ka la long ha Jerusalem ha ka snem 50 H.K. ban iakrcn shaphang ka jingpdiang ia ki Jentil sha ka Niam Khristan. Hadlcn nangne pat kaba kham bun ba ngi iah ban lip ka long na u Paul bad ka jingtrei Jong u. I . Ka jingim u Paul ha shiiwa ka jingkylla kaba nuit jong ti : U Saul u la long u khun kawei ka Jiw na Tarsos. U kpa Jong u u la long u trai shnong Rom da kaba thied, u long ruh u nongshna iingjain. Kumta kum u khynnah Jiw u la san u la rangbah ha ki Hukum ki Jiw, bad u la tip bha ia ki aifi ki dustur ki Jiw. Khlem pep u kpa bad ka kmie Jong u ki la hikai la iaiam ia u ba un minot, bad wat ban spel lyndet ruh ia ki Hukum bad ki kitab ki Hukum. La hikai ruh ia u da ki Nongtlioh bud ki Lebi ha ka Synagog hangta ha Tarsos. Hadicn pat u ia leit sa sha ka skul Grik, ha kaba la hikai bad la iathuh ha u ia ka Hislori ka Jingim jong ki riewradbah ki Grik, bad ka Niam Jong ki. Haba u la khum san kham samla, u kpa Jong u urn sngewhun ia u Saul ban pyntbit tang ha kinc ki skul rit ; kumta la leit buh ia u sha Jerusalem ban shong ha ki kjat uwei u nonghikai ba pawnam uba kyrteng u Gamaliel. Lyngbajong unc, u Saiil ii la san sha ka Jingstad bad ka Jingtip ban im ka Jingim kaba bniah bad kaba pyrkhing ha ka dur ki Pharisi. Dei nu kanc ka daw ba ha kawei ka sngi haba ki la lynthem maw ia ii Stephan, ba ma u ruh u ia iashong- shit lem ban pyniap ia u. 109 Ka kynhun kaba la khih pyrshah ban lynthem maw la u Stephan ka la rai ban pynshitom bad ban pyniap ia kito baroh kiba ialap bad kiba ngcit ia U Jisu Khrist, ha Jerusalem bad ha ki shnong kiba marjan. Ki ia iohi ruh ia ka jinglong jong u Saul ba u iapyrshah eh ia ka jinghikai ki Apostol. Kumta u Saul u la pan ka shitbi iohbor ban leit sha Damaskos na ka bynta ban pynshitom ia kito baroh kiba ngeit ha Jerusalem kiba ia phet noh sha Damaskos. Hynrei ha lynti u la iohi ia ka jingithuhpaw ba L) Trai Jisu hi U la paw ha u ; bad hangnc u Saul u la kloi ban ong, “Aiu Me mon ia nga ban leh ?”. U la shong matlah katto katne sngi, nangta u la iohi mat pat bad u la kylla kaba mut kaba thymmai kum u atiar ba kordor ch jong U Trai Jisu. U Paul u la long u Apostol ki .lentil. U la leit shong ha ri khlaw katto katne por. Ynda u la mih nangta u la sdang ban ialap ia U Jisu ia Uba u la pynshitom beifi ba U long U Nongpynim ka Pyrthci. 2. Ka Jingleil mishonari ii Paul: Ha ki snem ka jingleit ialap u Paul dci ii Nero uba long u Patsha ha Rom (54-68 H.K) bad u Philiks pat u long u Lyngskor ha Judia (.52-59 H.K). U Paul u la leit ialap kumba saw nc san sien lada khein bad kaba u leit sha Rom ba la kcm ia u ban iaiam ha khmat u Patsha Rom. Hangne ngin iapcit lyngkot ia baroh ki por ba u la leit ialap. (I) Ka jingleit ialap kaba nyngkong u Paul, u Barnabas lem bad u Joannis Markos (Ki Kan 13-14) kumba arsnem (47-49 H.K.). Ki la mil) na Antiok Syria ki da iaid lait ia ka dewlynnong Kypros. Ha .Salamis ki la ialap hapoh ka Synagog ki Jiw, bad nangta ki la poi sha Paphos. Hangne ki la iakynduh ia u Elimas u nonglehbyrtong bad ki la pynkylla Khristan ruh ia u Sergios Paulos. Na Paphos ki la leit da ka lieng sha Perga kaba ha Pamphilia bad nangne u loannis Markos u la leit phai noh sha la shnong. Nangta ki la leit sha Antiok no Pissidia bad ki la ialap hapoh ka Synagog ki Jiw. Kila poi pat sha Ikonnium ki da ialap shlur ; kumta la byrngem ban lynthem maw ia ki. Ki la iaphet noh nangta sha Lystra bad u Paul u la pynkhiah ia u briew uba dkob. Ki briew ki la kbot Jupiter ia u Barnabas bad Merkuri ia u Paul. La lynthem maw ia u Paul bad la leit bret ia u shabar shnong da kaba pyrkhat ba u la iap. Na Lystra ki la leit sha Derbi bad nan^a ki leit phai noh najuh na Lystra sha Ikonnium, Antiok Pissidia, Perga, Attalia bad da ka lieng sha Antiok Syria. Hapdeng ka jingleit kaba nyngkong bad kaba ar la pynlong ia ka Durbar Khristan kaba nyn^ong ha Jerusalem (SO H.K.), ha kaba la iakut ba lah ban pdiang ia ki Jentil lada khlera otsher ruh (ki Kam 15:1-35). La aibor ia u Paul bad u Barnabas ban leit biang sha ki Jentil. Haba ki la khreh ban leit biang u Barnabas u mon ban ialam biang ia u loannis Markos, hynrei u Paul um mon na ka daw ba u la phet noh ha ka jingleit kaba nyngkong. Kumta u Paul u la shim lok da u Silas bad ki la iakhlad noh bad u Barnabas. (2) Ka jingleit ialap kaba ar u Paul bad u Silas kumba lai snem (50-52 H.K.) Pule Ki Kam 15-18. Ki la iamih na Antiok Syria bad ki leit beit shaphang shatei sha Silikia, nangta ki poi sha Derbi bad Lystra. Ha Lystra la otsher ia u Timothi. Nangta pat ki la poi sha Ikonnium bad sha ri Phrygia, Pamphilia bad Pissidia nangta shaduh ri Galatia. Ha ri Galatia u Paul u la iohpang (Gal. 4:13). U Paul u la mut ban ialap han^o hynrei U Mynsiem U Blei Um shah ia u. Kumta ki la leit sha Mysia, Bethania bad sha Troas. Ha Troas u Paul u iohi ka jingithuhpaw ba uwei u briew na sha Makedonia u khot ia u, bad u ia sngewthuh ba ka dei ka jingphah U Blei ba u dei ban rung shapoh Europe. Kumta ki la leit sha Samothraki, sha Nea- polis bad sha Philipi — Ka Philipi ka dei ka jaka ba buhai shnong ki nong-Rom. Hangne u Paul, (1) u la pynkylla Ill Khristaa ia ka Lydia, (2) u la beh noh ia u ksuid na kawei ka samla. (3) La ring ia la ha kbmat ki majistor bad la sympat ia ki. La set byndi ia ki hynrei u Angel u la pyllait ia Id. (4) La pynkylla Khristan ia uta u nongap lingbyndi. Nangne u Paul, u Silas bad u Timothi ki leit poi sha Thessaloni ki da iaid na ka surok Egnatia lyngba ka Amphi- polis bad ka Appolonia. Ha Thessaloni la seng ia ka Balang, bad ki la iaiap lai sngi Sabbaton hapoh ka S^agog. U Paul u sah ha ling u Jason, hynrei namar ka jingkluhudn u paidbah u Paul u la phet noh sha Beria u da iehnoh ia u Silas bad u Timothi ha Thessaloni. Na Beria u Paul u leit sha Athen bad nangta sha Korinth. Ha Korinth u la seng Balang bad u la sah arsnem namar ba u pang ha ling u Akwila bad ka Priskila. Nangne u la thoh ia ki shithi 2 tylli sha ki nong-Thessaloni. Da ka jingsumar ba bha jong u Akwila bad ka Priskila u la koit pat bad u iehnoh ia ka Balang Korinth ha ka jingsumar jong ki, katba ia lade u leit phai sha Kenkhria, sha Ephesos bad sha Kaisaria. Ynda u la iakhublei ia ki Khristan hangto u la leit sha Jerusalem bad nangta sha Antiok Syria. (3) Ka jingleit iaiap kaba lai u Paul, u Timothi bad u Silas (Ki Kam 18:23—21:17) kumba lai nesaw snem (53-56 H.K.). Ki jinghikai ha khant kongsan u Paul ha ki Shithi Jong u : U Paul u la long u nongialap uba khraw, u nongseng Balang, u nonghikai bad kumjuh ruh u nongthoh shithi uba jur. Une ‘Uwei U Blei’ la ong ba U long U Kpa jong U Trai Jisu ‘Khrist.’ Hapdeng jong ngi bad U Blei don uwei u ksiang uba long u Briew Jisu Khrist Uba la aiti ia lade ban long ka Jingsiewspah ia baroh (I Tim. 2:5-6). U Mynsiem Bakhuid U wan ban trei ia ka kam u khun ban ai ia ki jingai ba kynja mvnsiem baroh (Rom 8:14-17 ; Gal. 5-16-25 ; II Kor. 1:21-22 ; etc). (2) Shaphang ka pop bad ka jingsiewspah. Naraar ka pop la wallara ia ka jing- bitar 1) Blei ha ki Jiw bad ki lentil ruh kumjuh. (3) Ka jingim kaba thymmai ha U Khrist. Ka jingpynksan da ka jingngeit ha ka jingiap U Jisu Khrist ka ialam sha ka jingpynthymmai ka jingim da ka jingiasoh bad U Khrist Uba im (Rom 6:1-11). KA KITAB KA RUTH Ka Kitab ka Ruth ka long kawei na ki Kitab Histori kaba itynnad ; ka iathuh ha ngi ia ka rukom im bad ka dustur ki riewhyndai. Ka iathuh ia ka jin^ong jong ka Ruth, ka Orpah bad ka Naomi. N^ iohi ia ka jinglong ka Oipah kaba la leit bud shiteng lynti ia la ka kiaw-kurim, hynrei ynda ka la doh ia ka, ka la wan phai noh sha la shnong; katba ka Ruth pat ka la kut jingmut ban bud ia la ka kiaw- kurim la im la iap. Na ka jin^ong ka Naomi ruh ngi iohi kumno ba ka shah ia Id jingjynjar, bad ba ka lah ban jop ia ka jingieit ki pyrsa-kurim jong ka. Ki ktien ba ka Ruth ka la krmi ki long kiba kordor: *‘Hangno 140 ba pha leit nga ruh ngan leit, hangno ba pha sah nga rub ngan sah, ki briew jong pha ki long ruh ki briew jong nga, U Blei jong pha U long ruh U Blei jong nga, hangno ba pha lap nga ruh ngan lap”. Haba pelt bha ia ka khana kaba don ha kane ka Kitab i kumba la thoh ia ka la slem bah, hynrei ki riewstad kiba peit bniah ia ka rukom thoh bad kiwei ki la shem ba la thoh ia kane ka Kitab hamar ka jinglong mraw ha Babilon lane kham hadien shuh shuh. Ka long kaba itynnad ban iohi ba u Mathaios u nong- thoh Gospel u thoh ia ka jinghiar pateng U Jisu da kaba ong ba u Boas u la pynkha ia u Obed na ka Ruth bad kumta ter ter haduh U Jisu. U Loukas ruh u mynjur kumjuh da kaba ong ba u Boas u pynkha ia u Obed bad u Obed ia u Jesse ter ter haduh U Jisu Khrist. Lada kumta kane ka Kitab ka long kaba kordor namar ka iathuh ha ngi ia ki kmeirad kparad tymmen jong U Trai Jisu — u Boas bad ka Ruth. Kane ka Kitab ka don ki jingmut ba kynja mynsiem. Ka Synduk ka Jutang bad ka jir^long lyngdoh : Ha ki Kitab u Samuel ka Synduk ka Jutang ka pyni ba ka long ka jaka shong U Blei, namar hangno ^ ka don hangta U Blei U don (Josh. 3, 4, 6,; Nongbishar 20:27). Ki lyngdoh ki dei ki briew (Nongbishar 17, 18) kiba la pynkyntang khamtam na ka bynta ka jingmane bad ka jingsumar ia ki mar ba kyntang jong ka Tempi. Kane ka kyrteng Messaiah ruh ka la paw nyngkong ha ka Kitab u Samuel (I Sam. 2:10). Ki lyng- doh ha kawei pat ka liang kum ki nongiathiihlypa ki leog ha ka jingiadei bad Id syiem, kumta namar ba u Saul 14S u kfiia hi ha Gilgal la pyorem ia u (I Sam. 13:8). KA KITAB U JOB HADUH KA JINGRWAI U SOLOMON : KA KITAB U JOB. 1. Ka kyrteng bad ka Kitab : Ka Kitab u Job ka long kawei na ki Kitab ba la khot *Ki Kitab Jingrwai*. La khot ruh ia ki *Ki Kitab Jingstad* 157 namar la thoh ha ki ia Id jingstad (wisdom) ha ka rukom jingrwai (Poe^). Kane ka Kitab u Job ka loag kawei na ki Kitab Idba kordor eh jong ka Baibl. U Victor Hugo u ong, ”Ka Kitab u Job ka long ka jingtei ba kordw eb jong u nongthoh uba stad, ka Tong Imba khrawtam late la mih na ka bor pyrkhat ba kynja briew”. U Thomas Carlyle pat u ong, “Nga khot ia ^e ka Kitab kate kyipang na ki jinghikai baroh kiba don, kawei na ki iii^ thoh kite khraw tarn ba la thoh ka long ka khana late rim tarn ia ka jingshah jynjar bym lah shun ban tetai. Ka jingshempap jong uba hok bad ka lynti U Blei ia ki briew baroh na kane ka pyrthei. Ym don kawei pat ka jingdioh nga tharai ka ban iaryngkat dor bad ka”. 2. Ka Ri Us : Ka ri Us (1 :1) la tharai ba ka don hamar ki pud jong ka ri Palestain ted ka ri Arabia. Ka iar naduh Edom sha* tei haduh ka wah luphratis stethie. Ka jaka shong u Job kat kum ka khana pateng la ong ba ka dei ka Haran, ka ri mihngi na Duriaw Galilaia, ka jaka kate seisoh shibun bad ka la long shisien ka jaka kaba bun briew. La ong ba haduh mynta la shem ba don 300 ki nongbah kite la jot . La don bun kite ngeit ba kata ka jaka ka dei ka ri Us. 3. Shaphang u Job, u nongthoh bad ka por ba la thoh ia kant ka Kitab : Don ka jingeh ten ngeit ba ka Kitab u Job ka kmg ka histori kaba shisha, ne kate sbu thaw kum ka kynja pharshi. Hapdeng ki Jiw don kiba ngeit ba ka da long sm- sha, don pat kite ong ba ka long ka jingthoh kate la shu mutdur. U Rabbi Lakish u ong, “U Job um don bad ym shym la thaw ia u, u long ka pharshi”. U Nongthoh bad ka par ba la thoh ia ka Kitab : Lah ban j^nshisha ba dd u Solomon uba la thoh ia kane ka Kitab (a) na ka rukom thoh, ka sur kien ; (b) ba 168 Q nongthoh u la ong, “Nga la lon^ u Syiem (1 :12) ; (k) u iathuh rub ia ki syiem kiba hadien jong u ; (d) u ong ba u la long syiem ha Jerusalem ; (e) ka jingthala ^ ka por jong a ka la pynlong ia u ba un thoh ia kane ka Kitab. Ka dur Jong kane ka Kitab : Ka sobjekt kaba khraw kane ka Kitab ka long ka Ving- thaia'. U nongthoh u tyrwa ia ki buit bad ki jingainia ha pyrshah ki jingthala. Kumta lah ban buh lyngkot ia ka dur jong ka kumne : — (a) Ha ki Kitab baroh U Blei U kren ne U pynpaw ha u briew, paidbah ne marwei, hynrei hangne U Blei U long Uba buhiieh ia lade, bad la dei ban ialeh jur ban shem ia U. Ha kane ka Kitab pat la kdew ba U Blei U long tang U Nong- bishar bad ym lah ban shem ia ka jingieit, jingisnei bad jingmap na U. (k) Ha kane ka Kitab la thoh tang ia ka liang ba iong ba dum ka pop u briew, ym shym kdew tang khyndiat run ia ki jingbha ha u briew : *Baroh ka long kaba thaia". Kumta kane ka Kitab ka iapher bak na kiwei pat ki Kitab. La katta ruh ym lah ban len ia ki jingtukai kane ka Kitab, ba u briew uba ia sop da ka jingsniew jingdum jingkordit, un mihpat uba la ioh khiah khran da ka jingieit bah U Blei kaba ha U Jisu Khrist. 4 . Ki jingjia hapdeng ka Shithi kaba Nyngkong bad kabaAr: (a) Ka jingpdiang ia ka Shithi kaba nyngkong da ka Balang Korinth — Kumba la kdew ha ka Shithi kaba nyngkong, u Paul namar bun ki daw u la phah ia u Timothi, nangta u la thoh ia ka Shithi ba nyngkong sha ki Nong-Korinth u da phah ruh ia u Titos ban lum ia ki jingkynshew. Kumta u Paul u la leit sha Korinth ban ring pat ia ki Khristan sha ki jinghikai kiba shisha. Kane ka jingleit U Paul ym shym kdew satia ha ki Kam ki Apostol; katba ha kane ka Shithi la pyni ba u la leit; hynrei la ong ba ki nongialam ki kynhun kim pdiang ia u (12:7-10), bad U la ialeh pyrshah ia u, namar kata u la leit phai noh sha Ephesos. (d) Kajingphahia u Titos bad ka shithi “kaba eh”— Na Ephesos u Paul u la thoh sa kawei ka shithi kaba kham eh (2: 3, 4; 7:8). La thoh ia ka ha ka dur kaba eh bad kaba sngew- sih ban khot ia ki sha ka jingkylla kaba mut. Ia kane ka Shithi la ong ba la kynthup ia M Lynnong 10-13 kane ka Shithi. Ha kane ka Shithi imat la kren Jur ia ka jinglong bad ka jing- iatiplem Jong ki.
